## General Drivers for RTD Collector


<article
            className="nested2"
            aria-labelledby="ariaid-title3"
            id="untitled16"
          >
            


### OPC DA


<div>
              <p>
                OPC DA protocol driver is to connect and collect data from
                devices that communicate based on OPC DA protocol, a standard
                protocol for industrial communication that enables efficient
                interconnection of heterogeneous systems.
              </p>
              <section className="section">
                <div className="note note_note" id="untitled16__note_jtm_qcz_vtb" >
                  <span className="note__title">Note:</span> When the OPC client
                  (i.e. collector) and the connected OPC server are not on the
                  same computer, you need to configure DCOM before making a
                  remote connection to OPC. Please refer to
                  <em>DCOM Configuration Manual </em>for DCOM configuration
                  before connection.
                </div>
              </section>
            </div>
            <article
              className="nested3"
              aria-labelledby="add_origin__title_sf1_4jj_25b"
              id="add_origin"
            >
              <h4 className="topictitle4" id="add_origin__title_sf1_4jj_25b">
                Adding Source
              </h4>
              <div>
                <section
                  className="section"
                  id="add_origin__context_ukk_v3m_wtb"
                />
                <section id="add_origin__steps_vkk_v3m_wtb">
                  <ol id="add_origin__steps_vkk_v3m_wtb">
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>Click <strong>Add</strong> on{" "}
                        <strong>Source</strong> page to expand
                        source information.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Enter source name and description, and select OPC DA for
                        driver name. The system expands the information that
                        needs to be entered for this driver according to the
                        selected driver.{" "}
                      </span>
                      <div>
                        <table id="add_origin__table_l5j_yhm_wtb">
                          <caption>
                            <span className="table--title-label">
                              Table 1.{" "}
                            </span>
                            <span>OPC DA source parameter specification</span>
                          </caption>
                          <colgroup><col style={{ width: "20%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "20%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "60%" }} /></colgroup>
                          <tbody>
                            <tr>
                              <td>Parameter</td>
                              <td>Definition</td>
                              <td>Description</td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td>Breakage Reconnection</td>
                              <td>
                                The reconnection mode when OPC Client and OPC
                                Server are disconnected.
                              </td>
                              <td>
                                <p>
                                  Reconnect: Reconnect only when OPC server is
                                  disconnected abnormally.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  Never reconnect: OPC server does not reconnect
                                  after disconnection.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  Always Reconnect: Reconnects when the OPC
                                  server is abnormally disconnected or normally
                                  exits.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td>Reconnection Interval</td>
                              <td>The time interval between two connections</td>
                              <td>
                                Selectable from 30, 60, 120, 300, 600, in
                                seconds
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td>Quality Code</td>
                              <td>User-defined quality code</td>
                              <td>
                                <p>
                                  One or more user-defined quality codes can be
                                  entered; if there are more than one, the
                                  different quality codes are separated by a
                                  slash. Such as 192, 192/216, 192/111/160, etc.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  If the quality code sent to the collector from
                                  OPC Server is among the above custom quality
                                  codes, the status code of the attribute value
                                  in the object instance will be displayed as 0
                                  after it is sent to supOS from the collector.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  If the quality code sent by OPC Server is
                                  different from that defined on the collector,
                                  for example, the collector quality code is
                                  customized to 192, and the quality code
                                  actually sent to the collector is 111, then
                                  the status code of the property value in supOS
                                  object instance is 200000000000000,
                                  representing abnormal data quality.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td>Clock Source</td>
                              <td>Timestamps used for data updates</td>
                              <td>
                                <ul id="add_origin__ul_or5_xr2_wtb">
                                  <li>
                                    <p>
                                      Local time: the timestamp of real-time
                                      data is computer time where the collector
                                      is located.
                                    </p>
                                  </li>
                                  <li>
                                    {" "}
                                    OPC server time: the timestamp of the
                                    real-time data is the time on the computer
                                    where the OPC server is located.
                                  </li>
                                </ul>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td>Request Delay</td>
                              <td>Request delay time</td>
                              <td>
                                <div className="p">
                                  <ul id="add_origin__ul_kxx_dsm_wtb">
                                    <li>
                                      Local time: the timestamp of real-time
                                      data is the time on the computer where the
                                      collector is located.
                                    </li>
                                    <li>
                                      OPC server time: the timestamp of the
                                      real-time data is the time on the computer
                                      where the OPC server is located.
                                    </li>
                                  </ul>
                                </div>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td>Authorization Settings</td>
                              <td>OPC UA server authorization </td>
                              <td>
                                <ul id="add_origin__ul_wkw_bsg_wtb">
                                  <li>
                                    If OPC UA server does not set user name and
                                    password, select anonymous to connect.
                                  </li>
                                  <li>
                                    {" "}
                                    If OPC UA server sets user name and
                                    password, you need to enter the
                                    corresponding user name and password.
                                  </li>
                                </ul>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td>Security Settings</td>
                              <td />
                              <td>
                                Encrypted data transmission is supported between
                                the collector and OPC UA server, and the
                                encryption methods are None (no encryption),
                                Sign, Sign &amp; Encrypt.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td>Security Mode</td>
                              <td>Set OPC UA driver encryption mode</td>
                              <td>
                                <p>
                                  When the security mode is None, there is no
                                  need to select a security policy.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  Other encryption methods can choose 4 security
                                  policies: Basic256, Basic128Rsa15,
                                  Basic256Sha256, Aes128Sha256RsaOaep.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td>Update Speed</td>
                              <td>Update speed of tag value</td>
                              <td>
                                Configure update rate. (range: 100-5000ms)
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td>Active Reading</td>
                              <td>Active reading configuration</td>
                              <td>
                                After being enabled, the data is read actively.
                                The device will periodically read all
                                successfully subscribed tags synchronously.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td>*OPC Server</td>
                              <td>OPC server information</td>
                              <td>
                                <p>
                                  Click <strong>Configure</strong> to expand the information that needs to be
                                  entered for the OPC server. After the
                                  information is entered, the system
                                  automatically generates the OPC server
                                  information in the format of OPC Service
                                  Address/OPC DA Service.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  {" "}
                                  The round light on the right side of the
                                  current OPC server is green.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td>*OPC Server Address</td>
                              <td>IP address of OPC server</td>
                              <td>-</td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td>*OPC Server Path</td>
                              <td>OPC DA server path</td>
                              <td>
                                Displays a list of all OPC services on the OPC
                                server, from which you can select the OPC DA
                                service you need to connect to.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td>Security Strategy</td>
                              <td>Active data reading settings</td>
                              <td>
                                When enabled, the data is read actively. And the
                                device will periodically read all successfully
                                subscribed tags synchronously{" "}
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td>DCOM Username/DCOM Password</td>
                              <td>DCOM username and password of OPC server</td>
                              <td>
                                If the OPC server login account is different
                                from the collector server login account, you
                                need to configure the DCOM username and password
                                of the OPC server.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td>Redundancy Configuration</td>
                              <td>Whether to start redundant OPC Server</td>
                              <td>
                                <p>
                                  The collector supports reading data from the
                                  redundant OPC Server.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  The collector can communicate with the
                                  redundant OPC server. When one OPC Server
                                  fails, it automatically switches to the
                                  non-failed OPC Server to continue
                                  communication. When both the master and slave
                                  OPC server fail, communication with the OPC
                                  Server is interrupted; and when one of them
                                  returns to normal, communication is
                                  automatically restored.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  The items to be configured are the same as the
                                  master OPC Server.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                          </tbody>
                        </table>
                      </div>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Select mode of breakage reconnection, the default is{" "}
                        <strong>
                       Reconnect after Disconnection </strong>
                        .{" "}
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span> Select the reconnection interval to be 30s.</span>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span> Enter custom quality code.</span>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span> Select local time for clock source. </span>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span> Set the request delay as 5s. </span>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span> Set the update speed to 1000ms.</span>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Configure</strong>{" "}
                        following OPC server and unfold the information that
                        need to be entered for OPC server.
                      </span>
                      <div>
                        <p>
                          a. You need to enter the IP address of OPC server that
                          you need to connect to. For example, 10.13.156.21
                        </p>
                        <p>
                          b. If the login accounts of OPC server and collector
                          server are different, you need to enter the DCOM user
                          name and password of OPC server.
                        </p>
                        <p>
                          {" "}
                          Click <strong>
                         Refresh List </strong>
                          following the OPC service address.
                        </p>
                        <p>
                          The corresponding OPC DA service list is automatically
                          displayed in the OPC Server path after refresh. Select
                          the required service among them.
                        </p>
                      </div>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        If you need to configure a redundant OPC DA server,
                        click{" "}
                        <strong>
                       Redundancy Configuration </strong>
                        and configure the parameters of the redundant OPC DA
                        server.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Save</strong> to
                        complete configuration.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                  </ol>
                </section>
              </div>
            </article>
            <article
              className="nested3"
              aria-labelledby="opc_da_import_tag__title_fps_4jj_25b"
              id="opc_da_import_tag"
            >
              <h4
                className="topictitle4"
                id="opc_da_import_tag__title_fps_4jj_25b"
              >
                Importing Tag
              </h4>
              <div>
                <p>
                  OPC DA driver supports batch import. After you have configured
                  the source, click <strong> Import tags in batch</strong> to
                  expand information of tag bulk import.
                  <img
                    id="opc_da_import_tag__image_u3y_1m4_35b"
                    src="https://wordpressfreezonex.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/supCollector/import.png"
                  />
                </p>
                <section className="section">
                  <div className="p">
                    <table
                      id="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb"
                      className="frame-all"
                    >
                      <caption />
                      <colgroup><col style={{ width: "20%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "20%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "60%" }} /></colgroup>
                      <thead>
                        <tr>
                          <th id="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__1">
                            Parameter
                          </th>
                          <th id="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__2">
                            Meaning
                          </th>
                          <th id="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__3">
                            Description
                          </th>
                        </tr>
                      </thead>
                      <tbody>
                        <tr>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__1">
                            (Synchronization)
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__2">
                            Incremental Synchronize of tag
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__3">
                            Synchronize tag information from OPC Server, in the
                            range of the incremental part. Time is re;atively
                            shorter, and the information may not be complete.
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__1">
                            (Full Synchronization)
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__2">
                            Full synchronization of tag
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__3">
                            Synchronize tag information in the range of all.
                            This may take longer time to complete.
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__1">
                            Add Prefix to Name
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__2">
                            Add prefix
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__3">
                            If the prefix is filled in, the prefix is added to
                            the selected tag when the tag is imported; if not,
                            no prefix is added.{" "}
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__1">
                            String Replacement
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__2">
                            Bulk replacement{" "}
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__3">
                            <ul id="opc_da_import_tag__ul_jf5_j5m_wtb">
                              <li>
                                {" "}
                                The replacement conditions can be deleted and
                                added, and the filter conditions can be
                                increased to a maximum of 4 and a minimum of 1.
                              </li>
                              <li>
                                {" "}
                                If characters are written in the original
                                character input box, the replacement are
                                performed; if no characters are filled in the
                                original character input box, the no replacement
                                are performed.
                              </li>
                            </ul>
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__1">
                            Intercept Tag Name
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__2">
                            Intercept Tag Name
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__3">
                            <p>
                              Intercept a segment of characters as a tag name
                              based on the specified intercept characters (the
                              separator). The interception is done from right to
                              left in reverse order.
                            </p>
                            <p>
                              Example: The original tag is named
                              <em>abc&amp;qvs&amp;wer</em>, the specified
                              intercept character is set to &amp;, and the
                              intercepted paragraph is set to 0-1 (backward),
                              then the intercepted tag name is
                              <em>wer</em>; intercept paragraph set 1-2
                              paragraphs (countdown), then the intercepted tag
                              name is
                              <em>qvs</em>.
                            </p>
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__1">
                            Read &amp; Write Status
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__2">
                            Set the read &amp; write status device tag
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__3">
                            If supOS is set to read/write, data can be written
                            down to the data source through the collector. If
                            supOS is set to read only, data cannot be written
                            down.
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__1">
                            Other Configuration
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__2">
                            Unfold detailed configuration item.
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__3">
                            -
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__1">
                            Unit Mode
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__2">
                            Set unit mode
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__3">
                            User-defined: Input unit manually.
                            <p>
                              From OPC server: units are automatically filled
                              with the OPC data source unit field name.
                            </p>
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__1">
                            Unit
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__2">
                            Tag unit
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__3">
                            Tag unit should be in accordance with OPC data
                            source.
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__1">
                            Range Mode
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__2">
                            Set range mode
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__3">
                            User-defined: Input upper and lower range limit
                            manually.
                            <p>
                              From OPC server: The upper and lower limit of
                              ranges are automatically filled with data
                              corresponding to OPC data source.
                            </p>
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__1">
                            Range Max
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__2">
                            Set range upper limit
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__3">
                            Set according to tag requirements. The default value
                            is 100.
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__1">
                            Range Min
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__2">
                            Set range lower limit
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__3">
                            Set range mode limit according to tag requirements.
                            The default value is 0.
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__1">
                            Description Mode
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__2">
                            Set description mode
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__3">
                            User-defined: Enter description manually.{" "}
                            <p>
                              According to OPC server: Description is
                              automatically filled with OPC data source
                              description field.
                            </p>
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__1">
                            Description
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__2">
                            Edit tag description
                          </td>
                          <td headers="opc_da_import_tag__table_lvp_j5m_wtb__entry__3">
                            Edit tag description.
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                      </tbody>
                    </table>
                  </div>
                </section>
                <section>
                  <ol>
                    <li>
                      <span>
                        Click <strong>Synchronize</strong> or{" "}
                        <strong>Fullsync</strong> to
                        synchronize information from source and enumerate tags
                        that have been synchronized to the list.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                      <span>
                        You can select tag to edit the parameter of the selected
                        tag.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                      <span>
                        Choose the tag to be imported, and click{" "}
                        <strong>Import to Tag</strong>.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                      <span>
                        The imported tags are displayed on{" "}
                        <strong>Tag</strong> page.{" "}
                      </span>
                    </li>
                  </ol>
                </section>
              </div>
            </article>
            <article
              className="nested3"
              aria-labelledby="untitled11__title_odc_pjj_25b"
              id="untitled11"
            >
              <h4 className="topictitle4" id="untitled11__title_odc_pjj_25b">
                Adding Tag
              </h4>
              <div>
                <p />
                <section className="section" />
                <section>
                  <ol>
                    <li>
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Add</strong> to unfold
                        basic properties of tag.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        After the basic properties are entered, the system
                        automatically adds relevant configuration properties for
                        the settings of connection point between tag and the
                        underlying data.{" "}
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Select</strong> to
                        unfold tag selection information.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Enter tag information in{" "}
                        <strong>Tag Search</strong> for fuzzy query or click refresh button, and the
                        optional tag will automatically display related items
                        according to the selected source.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click blue <strong>√</strong> after
                        selecting the corresponding tag, and the system
                        automatically displays I/O address.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Save</strong> to
                        complete configuration.
                        <img
                          id="untitled11__image_x2g_1gv_35b"
                          src="https://wordpressfreezonex.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/supCollector/tag%20search.png"
                        />
                      </span>
                    </li>
                  </ol>
                </section>

### OPC UA


<div>
              <p>
                OPC UA driver, mainly used to connect to OPC UA protocol-based
                servers for data acquisition.
              </p>
              <section className="section" />
            </div>
            <article
              className="nested3"
              aria-labelledby="untitled6__title_xkg_qjj_25b"
              id="untitled6"
            >
              <h4 className="topictitle4" id="untitled6__title_xkg_qjj_25b">
                Adding Source
              </h4>
              <div>
                <p />
                <section className="section" />
                <section>
                  <ol>
                    <li>
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Add</strong> on{" "}
                        <strong>Source</strong> to expand
                        source information.{" "}
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Enter source name and description, and select{" "}
                        <strong>OPC UA</strong> for driver name. The system expands the information that
                        needs to be entered for this driver according to the
                        selected driver.{" "}
                      </span>
                    </li>
                  </ol>
                  <div>
                    <table>
                      <caption>
                        <span className="table--title-label">Table 2. </span>
                        <span>OPC UA source point parameter specification</span>
                      </caption>
                      <colgroup><col style={{ width: "20%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "20%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "60%" }} /></colgroup>
                      <thead>
                        <tr>
                          <th id="untitled6__entry__1">Parameter</th>
                          <th id="untitled6__entry__2">Definition</th>
                          <th id="untitled6__entry__3">Description</th>
                        </tr>
                      </thead>
                      <tbody>
                        <tr>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__1">Clock Source</td>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__2">
                            Timestamp used for data updates
                          </td>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__3">
                            <ul id="untitled6__ul_or5_xr2_wtb">
                              <li>
                                <p>
                                  Local time: the timestamp of real-time data is
                                  the time on the computer where the collector
                                  is located.
                                </p>
                              </li>
                              <li>
                                {" "}
                                OPC server time: the timestamp of the real-time
                                data is the time on the computer where the OPC
                                server is located.
                              </li>
                            </ul>
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__1">
                            Breakage Reconnection
                          </td>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__2">
                            Reconnection mode when OPC Client and OPC Server are
                            disconnected.
                          </td>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__3">
                            <p>
                              Reconnection: Reconnect only when OPC server is
                              disconnected abnormal.
                            </p>
                            <p>
                              Never Reconnect: OPC server does not reconnect
                              after disconnection.
                            </p>
                            <p>
                              Always Reconnect: Reconnects when the OPC server
                              is abnormally disconnected or normally exits.
                            </p>
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__1">
                            Reconnection Interval
                          </td>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__2">
                            The time interval between two times of reconnection.
                          </td>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__3">
                            Selectable from 30, 60, 120, 300, 600, in seconds.
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__1">
                            Authorization Settings
                          </td>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__2">
                            OPC UA server authorization
                          </td>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__3">
                            <ul id="untitled6__ul_wkw_bsg_wtb">
                              <li>
                                If OPC UA server is not set username and
                                password, select anonymous to connect.
                              </li>
                              <li>
                                {" "}
                                If OPC UA server sets user name and password,
                                you need to enter the corresponding user name
                                and password to connect successfully.
                              </li>
                            </ul>
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__1">
                            Security Settings
                          </td>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__2">-</td>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__3">
                            Encrypted data transmission is supported between the
                            collector and OPC UA server, and the encryption
                            methods are None (no encryption), Sign, Sign &amp;
                            Encrypt.
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__1">Security Mode</td>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__2">
                            Set OPC UA driver encryption mode
                          </td>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__3">
                            <p>
                              When the security mode is None, there is no need
                              to select a security policy.
                            </p>
                            <p>
                              Other encryption methods can choose 4 security
                              policies: Basic256, Basic128Rsa15, Basic256Sha256,
                              and Aes128Sha256RsaOaep.
                            </p>
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__1">
                            Security Strategy
                          </td>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__2">
                            Active data reading settings
                          </td>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__3">
                            When enabled, the data is read actively. And the
                            device will periodically read all successfully
                            subscribed tag synchronously.
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__1">
                            Certificate File der Path
                          </td>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__2">
                            OPC server information
                          </td>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__3">
                            <p>
                              {" "}
                              Click{" "}
                              <strong>
                             Configuration </strong> to unfold the information that needs to be entered
                              for the OPC server. After the information is
                              entered, the system automatically generates the
                              OPC server information in the format of OPC
                              Service Address/OPC DA Service".
                            </p>
                            <p>
                              The round light on the right side of the currently
                              connected OPC server is green.
                            </p>
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__1">
                            Private Key File pem Path
                          </td>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__2">
                            IP address of OPC server
                          </td>
                          <td headers="untitled6__entry__3">-</td>
                        </tr>
                      </tbody>
                    </table>
                    <p />
                  </div>
                  <ol start={3}>
                    <li>
                      <span>
                        Enter the IP address of the OPC server you need to
                        connect to, for example: 10.13.156.21.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Select the breakage reconnection mode, and the default
                        is <strong>
                       Always Reconnect </strong>
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                      <span> Select a reconnection interval of 30s.</span>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Select <strong>Local Time </strong>as
                        the clock source.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Select the authorization mode according to the OPC UA
                        server settings.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Set the data encryption transmission method between the
                        collector and OPC UA server.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Save</strong>.
                      </span>
                    </li>

                </section>

              <h4 className="topictitle4" id="untitled7__title_q45_qjj_25b">
                Importing Tag
              </h4>
              <div>
                <p>
                  OPC UA driver supports batch import of tag. After you have
                  configured the source information, go to{" "}
                  <strong>Import tags in batch</strong> tab to
                  expand tag batch import information.
                </p>
                <section className="section">
                  <div className="p">
                    <table>
                      <caption />
                      <colgroup><col style={{ width: "20%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "20%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "60%" }} /></colgroup>
                      <tbody>
                        <tr>
                          <td>Parameter</td>
                          <td>Meaning</td>
                          <td>Description</td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td>(Synchronization)</td>
                          <td>Synchronize tag</td>
                          <td>
                            Synchronize tag information from OPC Server, in the
                            range of all
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td>(Enumerate tag)</td>
                          <td>Enumerate current tag</td>
                          <td>
                            Display all tag information of OPC DA data source
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td>String Replacement</td>
                          <td>Bulk replacement </td>
                          <td>
                            <ul>
                              <li>
                                {" "}
                                The replacement conditions can be deleted and
                                added, and the filter conditions can be
                                increased to a maximum of 4 and a minimum of 1.
                              </li>
                              <li>
                                {" "}
                                If characters are written in the original
                                character input box, the replacement will be
                                performed; if no characters are filled in the
                                original character input box, the no replacement
                                will be performed
                              </li>
                            </ul>
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td>Truncate the Tag Name</td>
                          <td>Truncate Tag Name</td>
                          <td>
                            <p>
                              Intercept a segment of characters as a tag name
                              based on the specified intercept characters as a
                              separator. The interception is done from right to
                              left in reverse order.
                            </p>
                            <p>
                              Example: The original tag is named
                              <em>abc&amp;qvs&amp;wer</em>, the specified
                              intercept character is set to <em>&amp;</em>, and
                              the intercepted paragraph is set to{" "}
                              <em>0-1 (backward)</em>, then the intercepted tag
                              name is
                              <em>wer</em>; If intercept paragraph is set to{" "}
                              <em>1-2 paragraphs (countdown)</em>, then the
                              intercepted tag name is <em>qvs</em>.
                            </p>
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td>Read &amp; Write Statua</td>
                          <td>Set the read &amp; write state equipment tag</td>
                          <td>
                            If supOS is set to read/write, data can be written
                            down to the data source through the collector. If
                            supOS is set to read only, data cannot be written
                            down.
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td>Other Configuration</td>
                          <td>Unfold detailed configuration page</td>
                          <td>-</td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td>Grouping</td>
                          <td>Tag grouping</td>
                          <td>
                            By default, the software establishes 128 groups from
                            0 to 127, you can manage the tag in groups according
                            to tag classification.
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td>Unit Mode</td>
                          <td>Set unit mode</td>
                          <td>
                            User-defined: Input unit manually.
                            <p>
                              From OPC server: units are automatically filled
                              with the OPC data source unit field name.
                            </p>
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td>Unit</td>
                          <td>Tag unit</td>
                          <td>
                            Tag unit should be in accordance with OPC data
                            source.
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td>Range Mode</td>
                          <td>Set range mode</td>
                          <td>
                            User-defined: Input upper and lower range limit
                            manually.
                            <p>
                              From OPC server: The upper and lower limit of
                              range are automatically filled with data
                              corresponding to OPC data source.
                            </p>
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td>Range Max</td>
                          <td>Set range upper limit</td>
                          <td>
                            Set according to tag requirements. The default value
                            is 100.
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td>Range Min</td>
                          <td>Set range lower limit</td>
                          <td>
                            Set according to tag requirements. The default value
                            is 0.
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td>Description Mode</td>
                          <td>Set description mode</td>
                          <td>
                            Customize: Input description manually.{" "}
                            <p>
                              From OPC server: Description is automatically
                              filled with OPC data source description field.
                            </p>
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr>
                          <td>Description</td>
                          <td>Edit tag description</td>
                          <td>Edit tag description information.</td>
                        </tr>
                      </tbody>
                    </table>
                  </div>
                </section>
                <section>
                  <ol>
                    <li>
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Enumerate Tags</strong>,
                        and the system will systematically enumerate tag
                        information corresponding to the source point. If a new
                        tag is added to the source, perform Synchronization
                        before tag enumeration.
                      </span>
                    </li>

                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        You can select tag to edit the parameter information of

                      </span>

### Modbus RTU


<div>
              <p>
                {" "}
                Modbus RTU protocol driver. The caller can implement the access
                to the standard Modbus RTU system.
              </p>
              <section className="section" />
            </div>
            <article
              className="nested3"
              aria-labelledby="untitled9__title_esz_tjj_25b"
              id="untitled9"
            >
              <h4 className="topictitle4" id="untitled9__title_esz_tjj_25b">
                Adding Source
              </h4>
              <div>
                <p />
                <section className="section" />
                <section>
                  <ol>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Add</strong> on{" "}
                        <strong>Source</strong> to expand
                        source information.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Enter source name and description, and select{" "}
                        <strong>Modbus RTU</strong> for driver
                        name. The system expands the information that needs to
                        be entered for this driver according to the selected
                        driver.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong> Channel</strong> to
                        add channels and configure channel parameters. Parameter
                        description is as follows.
                      </span>
                      <div>
                        <div className="p">
                          <table
                            id="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb"
                            className="frame-all"
                          >
                            <caption>
                              <span className="table--title-label">
                                Table 3.
                              </span>
                              <span>Channel parameter specification</span>
                            </caption>
                            <colgroup><col style={{ width: "20%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "20%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "60%" }} /></colgroup>
                            <thead>
                              <tr>
                                <th id="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__1">
                                  Parameter
                                </th>
                                <th id="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__2">
                                  Meaning
                                </th>
                                <th id="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__3">
                                  Description
                                </th>
                              </tr>
                            </thead>
                            <tbody>
                              <tr>
                                <td headers="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__1">
                                  Channel
                                </td>
                                <td headers="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__2">
                                  Channel
                                </td>
                                <td headers="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__3">
                                  -
                                </td>
                              </tr>
                              <tr>
                                <td headers="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__1">
                                  *Name
                                </td>
                                <td headers="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__2">
                                  -
                                </td>
                                <td headers="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__3">
                                  -
                                </td>
                              </tr>
                              <tr>
                                <td headers="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__1">
                                  Description
                                </td>
                                <td headers="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__2">
                                  -
                                </td>
                                <td headers="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__3">
                                  -
                                </td>
                              </tr>
                              <tr>
                                <td headers="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__1">
                                  *Serial Port
                                </td>
                                <td headers="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__2">
                                  Device number
                                </td>
                                <td headers="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__3">
                                  Device ID is unique, and must be the same with
                                  original device ID.
                                </td>
                              </tr>
                              <tr>
                                <td headers="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__1">
                                  *Baud Rate
                                </td>
                                <td headers="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__2">
                                  Baud rate of channel
                                </td>
                                <td headers="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__3">
                                  The settings must be consistent with the
                                  corresponding parameters of serial port of the
                                  other party.
                                </td>
                              </tr>
                              <tr>
                                <td headers="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__1">
                                  Stop Bit
                                </td>
                                <td headers="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__2">
                                  Time between transmission of each character,
                                  measured in bits per second.
                                </td>
                                <td headers="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__3">
                                  The optional parameters are 1, 1.5 and 2, and
                                  the default is 1. The settings must be
                                  consistent with the parameters corresponding
                                  to PLC.
                                </td>
                              </tr>
                              <tr>
                                <td headers="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__1">
                                  Parity
                                </td>
                                <td headers="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__2">
                                  Type of error checking for the port.
                                </td>
                                <td headers="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__3">
                                  <p>
                                    Optional parameters include the following:
                                  </p>
                                  <div className="p">
                                    <ul id="untitled9__ul_oy5_ph4_n5b">
                                      <li>
                                        None, indicating that no parity bit is
                                        added to data bits sent from this port.
                                      </li>
                                      <li>
                                        Odd, indicating that if the number of
                                        1's in the data bits is to be odd. The
                                        parity bit should be added.{" "}
                                      </li>
                                      <li>
                                        Even, indicating that if the number of
                                        1's in the data bits is to be even. The
                                        parity bit should be set to 1.
                                      </li>
                                      <li>
                                        Mark, meaning adding parity bit. (always
                                        set to 0).
                                      </li>
                                      <li>
                                        {" "}
                                        Space, meaning adding parity bit (always
                                        set to 1).
                                        <p>
                                          {" "}
                                          The settings must be consistent with
                                          the parameters corresponding to the
                                          serial port of the other party.
                                        </p>
                                      </li>
                                    </ul>
                                  </div>
                                </td>
                              </tr>
                              <tr>
                                <td headers="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__1">
                                  Stop Bit
                                </td>
                                <td headers="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__2">
                                  Time between transmission of each character,
                                  measured in bits per second.
                                </td>
                                <td headers="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__3">
                                  The optional parameters are 1and 2. The
                                  settings must be consistent with the
                                  parameters corresponding to the serial port of
                                  the other party.
                                </td>
                              </tr>
                              <tr>
                                <td headers="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__1">
                                  *Time-out Time
                                </td>
                                <td headers="untitled9__table_qbr_vyg_wtb__entry__2">
                                  The maximum waiting time between the command
                                  sent by the master and response{" "}
                                </td>

                              </td>

                                to be sent. (The default time is 5.)
                              </td>

                            <tr>
                              <td headers="modbus_tcp_add_origin__table_okv_tgm_wtb__entry__1">
                                Redundancy Configuration
                              </td>
                              <td headers="modbus_tcp_add_origin__table_okv_tgm_wtb__entry__2">
                                Whether to start redundant OPC Server
                              </td>
                              <td headers="modbus_tcp_add_origin__table_okv_tgm_wtb__entry__3">
                                <p>
                                  The collector supports reading data from the
                                  redundant OPC Server.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  The collector can communicate with the
                                  redundant OPC Server. When one OPC Server
                                  fails, it automatically switches to the
                                  non-failed OPC Server to continue
                                  communication. When both the master and slave
                                  OPC Server fail, communication with the OPC
                                  Server is interrupted, and when one of them
                                  returns to normal, communication is
                                  automatically restored.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  The items to be configured are the same as the
                                  master OPC Server.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                          </tbody>
                        </table>

                                -
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="kfdhakhg__table_zk3_xzm_wtb__entry__1">
                                *Address Length
                              </td>
                              <td headers="kfdhakhg__table_zk3_xzm_wtb__entry__2">
                                {" "}
                                The difference between the end address and the
                                start address.
                              </td>
                              <td headers="kfdhakhg__table_zk3_xzm_wtb__entry__3">
                                COIL, DISCRETES INPUT type address with a
                                maximum length of 2000, the minimum is 1; INPUT
                                REGISTER, HOLDING REGISTER type address with a
                                maximum length of 125, the minimum length of 1.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="kfdhakhg__table_zk3_xzm_wtb__entry__1">
                                Data Type
                              </td>
                              <td headers="kfdhakhg__table_zk3_xzm_wtb__entry__2">
                                Data type
                              </td>
                              <td headers="kfdhakhg__table_zk3_xzm_wtb__entry__3">
                                <p>
                                  Data type of data source, as well as
                                  forward/reverse order, byte swapping, etc.
                                </p>
                                <ul id="kfdhakhg__ul_vtg_cxm_wtb">
                                  <li>
                                    string: selection of encoding and string
                                    length.
                                  </li>
                                  <li>bool: bit setting</li>
                                  <li>short/unshort: AB/BA</li>
                                  <li>
                                    long/unlong/float: ABCD/CDBA/BADC/DCBA
                                  </li>
                                  <li>double: asc/decs</li>
                                  <li>byte/char: A/B</li>
                                </ul>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                          </tbody>
                        </table>
                      </div>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Enumerate Tags</strong>.
                        After you have selected the tags to be imported, click <strong> Import</strong> to import
                        tags.
                      </span>
                      <div>
                        <div className="p">
                          


:::info


please refer to <a href="untitled5.html#opc_da_import_tag__title_fps_4jj_25b">Importing Tag</a> for detailed operations on tag name (e.g. prefix adding, string swapping and intercepting).

:::

</div>
                      </div>
                    </li>
                  </ol>
                </section>
              </div>
            </article>
            <article
              className="nested3"
              aria-labelledby="modbus_tcp_add_tag__title_ccm_xjj_25b"
              id="modbus_tcp_add_tag"
            >
              <h4
                className="topictitle4"
                id="modbus_tcp_add_tag__title_ccm_xjj_25b"
              >
                Adding Tag
              </h4>
              <div>
                <section>
                  <ol>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Add</strong> to unfold
                        basic properties of tag.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        After the basic property content is input, the system
                        automatically adds the relevant configuration properties
                        for the connection point between tag and the underlying
                        data.{" "}
                      </span>
                      <div>
                        <img
                          id="modbus_tcp_add_tag__image_d3s_qk4_n5b"
                          src="https://wordpressfreezonex.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/supCollector/modbus%20TCP%20tag.png"
                        />
                      </div>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span> Select tag, for example, Device0.</span>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span> Enter address, ranging from 0 to 65535.</span>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Select function code and data type. (Refer to{" "}
                        <a href="untitled5.html#untitled10__title_rtj_5jj_25b">
                          Modbus RTU Importing Tag
                        </a>{" "}
                        for details.)
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">

                        {" "}

### DDE


<p>
              DDE is a dynamic data exchange (DDE) system. DDE uses a shared
              memory to exchange data between two applications.
            </p>
