### BACnet TCP/IP


<div>
              <p>
                BACnet driver is used for intelligent building communication.
                Find all BACnet servers in the same network segment as the IP
                address of the collector server by configuring the source. A
                collector can only create one valid BACnet source.
              </p>
              <section className="section" />
            </div>
            <article
              className="nested3"
              aria-labelledby="bacnet_tcp_ip_add_origin__title_dzw_zjj_25b"
              id="bacnet_tcp_ip_add_origin"
            >
              <h4
                className="topictitle4"
                id="bacnet_tcp_ip_add_origin__title_dzw_zjj_25b"
              >
                Adding Source
              </h4>
              <div>
                <p />
                <section>
                  <ol>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Add</strong> on{" "}
                        <strong>Source</strong> to expand
                        source information configuration.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Enter source name and description, and select{" "}
                        <strong>BACnet</strong> for the driver. The system expands the information that
                        needs to be entered for this driver according to the
                        selected driver.{" "}
                      </span>
                      <div>
                        <table
                          id="bacnet_tcp_ip_add_origin__table_ot5_vfn_wtb"
                          className="frame-all"
                        >
                          <caption>
                            <span className="table--title-label">Table 8.</span>
                            <span>BACnet source parameter specification</span>
                          </caption>
                          <colgroup>
                            <col style={{ width: "30%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "70%" }} />
                          </colgroup>
                          <thead>
                            <tr>
                              <th id="bacnet_tcp_ip_add_origin__table_ot5_vfn_wtb__entry__1">
                                Parameter
                              </th>
                              <th id="bacnet_tcp_ip_add_origin__table_ot5_vfn_wtb__entry__2">
                                Specification
                              </th>
                            </tr>
                          </thead>
                          <tbody>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="bacnet_tcp_ip_add_origin__table_ot5_vfn_wtb__entry__1">
                                <strong>Virtual Link Layer</strong>
                              </td>
                              <td headers="bacnet_tcp_ip_add_origin__table_ot5_vfn_wtb__entry__2">
                                Select BACnet IP by default to connect via IP
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="bacnet_tcp_ip_add_origin__table_ot5_vfn_wtb__entry__1">
                                *IP Address
                              </td>
                              <td headers="bacnet_tcp_ip_add_origin__table_ot5_vfn_wtb__entry__2">
                                Fill in the IP address of the collector software
                                server (local IP), IP address and subnet mask to
                                determine the BACnet device broadcast segment.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="bacnet_tcp_ip_add_origin__table_ot5_vfn_wtb__entry__1">
                                *Subnet Mask
                              </td>
                              <td headers="bacnet_tcp_ip_add_origin__table_ot5_vfn_wtb__entry__2">
                                Fill in the subnet mask of the collector
                                software server
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="bacnet_tcp_ip_add_origin__table_ot5_vfn_wtb__entry__1">
                                *Port
                              </td>
                              <td headers="bacnet_tcp_ip_add_origin__table_ot5_vfn_wtb__entry__2">
                                The default is 47808
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="bacnet_tcp_ip_add_origin__table_ot5_vfn_wtb__entry__1">
                                *Collect Interval
                              </td>
                              <td headers="bacnet_tcp_ip_add_origin__table_ot5_vfn_wtb__entry__2">
                                Set the data collection period in milliseconds
                                (The default is 1000 milliseconds).{" "}
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                          </tbody>
                        </table>
                      </div>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Save</strong> to
                        complete configuration.
                      </span>
                      <div>
                        


:::info


Since the BACnet driver also acts as a server and the default
                          port is 47808, a collector software can only create
                          one BACnet source.

:::

</div>
                    </li>
                  </ol>
                </section>
              </div>
            </article>

## National Standard


<article

### HJ212 2017


<div>
              <section className="section">
                <p>
                  Environment HJ212-2017 standard protocol, mainly used to
                  connect the data acquisition instrument ① that adopts the data
                  transmission standard of pollutant online monitoring
                  (monitoring) system.
                </p>
                <p>
                  Note ① Data Acquisition Devices: Data acquisition and
                  transmission devices that collect data from various types of
                  monitoring devices. These devices store, transmit and
                  communicate with the host computer micro-controller,
                  industrial control machine, embedded computer, programmable
                  automation controller (Programmable Automation Controller,
                  PAC) or programmable controller (PLC), etc., and are referred
                  to as Digital acquisition instrument.
                </p>
              </section>
            </div>
            <article
              className="nested3"
              aria-labelledby="hj212_add_origin__title_lxr_bkj_25b"
              id="hj212_add_origin"

                id="hj212_add_origin__title_lxr_bkj_25b"
              >
                Adding Source
              </h4>
              <div>
                <section>
                  <ol>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Add</strong> on{" "}
                        <strong>Source</strong>.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Enter source name and description, and select{" "}
                        <strong>HJ212 2017</strong> for the
                        driver. The system expands the information that needs to
                        be entered for this driver according to the selected
                        driver.

                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Enter basic properties, and select{" "}
                        <strong>HJ 212 2017</strong> for driver name. The system will automatically configure
                        attributes.
                      </span>
                      <div>
                        <table
                          id="hj212_add_tag__table_ycx_4ln_wtb"
                          className="frame-all"
                        >
                          <caption>
                            <span className="table--title-label">
                              Table 11.
                            </span>
                            <span>HJ212 2017 tag parameter specification</span>
                          </caption>
                          <colgroup>
                            <col style={{ width: "30%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "70%" }} />
                          </colgroup>
                          <thead>
                            <tr>
                              <th id="hj212_add_tag__table_ycx_4ln_wtb__entry__1">
                                Parameter
                              </th>
                              <th id="hj212_add_tag__table_ycx_4ln_wtb__entry__2">
                                Specification
                              </th>
                            </tr>
                          </thead>
                          <tbody>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="hj212_add_tag__table_ycx_4ln_wtb__entry__1">
                                *Device Unique Identification
                              </td>
                              <td headers="hj212_add_tag__table_ycx_4ln_wtb__entry__2">
                                The unique identification (MN) of the digital
                                mining instrument device, consistent with the
                                site identification.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="hj212_add_tag__table_ycx_4ln_wtb__entry__1">
                                *System Coding
                              </td>
                              <td headers="hj212_add_tag__table_ycx_4ln_wtb__entry__2">
                                Select system code.
                                <p>
                                  The system code is divided into four
                                  categories, each of which indicates a system
                                  type.
                                </p>
                                <div className="p">
                                  <ul id="hj212_add_tag__ul_msb_tmn_wtb">
                                    <li>
                                      10~29 indicate environmental quality
                                      categories.
                                    </li>
                                    <li>
                                      30~49 denote environmental pollution
                                      source categories.
                                    </li>
                                    <li>
                                      50~69 indicates the working condition
                                      category.
                                    </li>
                                    <li>
                                      91~99 indicates the system interaction
                                      category
                                    </li>
                                  </ul>
                                </div>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="hj212_add_tag__table_ycx_4ln_wtb__entry__1">
                                Command Encoding
                              </td>
                              <td headers="hj212_add_tag__table_ycx_4ln_wtb__entry__2">
                                <p>
                                  Select the command code. There are four
                                  categories of command codes.
                                </p>
                                <div className="p">
                                  <ul id="hj212_add_tag__ul_df3_zmn_wtb">
                                    <li>
                                      1000~1999 indicate initialization command
                                      and parameter command codes.
                                    </li>
                                    <li>
                                      2000~2999 indicates data command codes.
                                    </li>
                                    <li>
                                      3000~3999 indicates control command codes.
                                    </li>
                                    <li>
                                      9000~9999 indicates interactive command
                                      codes
                                    </li>
                                  </ul>
                                </div>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="hj212_add_tag__table_ycx_4ln_wtb__entry__1">
                                Query Interval
                              </td>
                              <td headers="hj212_add_tag__table_ycx_4ln_wtb__entry__2">
                                Time interval for the collector to actively
                                check the data.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="hj212_add_tag__table_ycx_4ln_wtb__entry__1">
                                *Target Field
                              </td>
                              <td headers="hj212_add_tag__table_ycx_4ln_wtb__entry__2">
                                Field name of data area.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="hj212_add_tag__table_ycx_4ln_wtb__entry__1">
                                Target Field Parameter
                              </td>
                              <td headers="hj212_add_tag__table_ycx_4ln_wtb__entry__2">
                                The value of xxxxxxx or xxx in the target field.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="hj212_add_tag__table_ycx_4ln_wtb__entry__1">
                                Custom Data Fields
                              </td>
                              <td headers="hj212_add_tag__table_ycx_4ln_wtb__entry__2">
                                <p>
                                  User-defined CP field value (without
                                  &amp;&amp;), some data need to be actively
                                  queried in time (It cannot be subscribed),
                                  this field as CP parameters passes in when
                                  query is requested. For example: the command
                                  code 3020 (to extract the information of the
                                  field machine) can be set to
                                  CP=&amp;&amp;PolId=w01018;
                                  InfoId=i12001&amp;&amp; in the data area when
                                  the request is initiated.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  The field is valid when the current command
                                  code is
                                  1011,1061,1063,3015,3017,3018,3019,3020.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                          </tbody>
                        </table>
                      </div>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Save</strong> to
                        complete the configuration.
                      </span>
                      <div>
                        


:::info


See <em>HJ212-2017 Data Transmission Standards for Pollutant Online Monitoring Systems</em> for detailed HJ212 2017 standard protocol information.

:::

</div>
                    </li>
                  </ol>
                </section>
              </div>
            </article>
          </article>

                                    </li>

                <section>
                  <ol>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Add</strong> to unfold
                        basic properties of tag.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        After the basic property content is input, the system
                        automatically adds the relevant configuration properties
                        for the connection point between tag and the underlying
                        data.
                      </span>
                      <div>
                        <img
                          id="dlt_645_add_tag__image_lvk_4m4_n5b"
                          src="https://wordpressfreezonex.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/supCollector/DLT6451.png"
                        />
                      </div>
                      <div>
                        <table
                          id="dlt_645_add_tag__table_mk2_kqn_wtb"
                          className="frame-all"
                        >
                          <caption>
                            <span className="table--title-label">
                              Table 17.
                            </span>
                            <span>
                              DLT645 related configuration specification
                            </span>
                          </caption>
                          <colgroup><col style={{ width: "20%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "20%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "60%" }} /></colgroup>
                          <thead>
                            <tr>
                              <th id="dlt_645_add_tag__table_mk2_kqn_wtb__entry__1">
                                Parameter
                              </th>
                              <th id="dlt_645_add_tag__table_mk2_kqn_wtb__entry__2">
                                Meaning
                              </th>

                                Description
                              </th>
                            </tr>
                          </thead>
                          <tbody>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="dlt_645_add_tag__table_mk2_kqn_wtb__entry__1">
                                *Device Address
                              </td>
                              <td headers="dlt_645_add_tag__table_mk2_kqn_wtb__entry__2">
                                Production address of ammeters.
                              </td>
                              <td headers="dlt_645_add_tag__table_mk2_kqn_wtb__entry__3">
                                Form: Device name /Ammeter address
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="dlt_645_add_tag__table_mk2_kqn_wtb__entry__1">
                                *Get Interval
                              </td>
                              <td headers="dlt_645_add_tag__table_mk2_kqn_wtb__entry__2">
                                Tine interval for obtaining power meter data.
                              </td>
                              <td headers="dlt_645_add_tag__table_mk2_kqn_wtb__entry__3">
                                Set the acquisition frequency in seconds.
                                (Default is 5s.)
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="dlt_645_add_tag__table_mk2_kqn_wtb__entry__1">
                                Data Identification
                              </td>
                              <td headers="dlt_645_add_tag__table_mk2_kqn_wtb__entry__2">
                                Data identification code identifies different
                                data items with 4 bytes.
                              </td>
                              <td headers="dlt_645_add_tag__table_mk2_kqn_wtb__entry__3">
                                See <a href="#dlt_645__title_sc4_ckj_25b">DL/T645-2007</a>
                                communication protocol for details.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                          </tbody>
                        </table>
                      </div>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Save</strong> to
                        complete configuration.
                      </span>

                                      Odd parity, which indicates that the
                                      parity bit should be set to 1 if the
                                      number of 1 in the data bits is to be odd.
                                    </li>

### SQL2DB


<div>
              <p>
                SQL to DB driver, mainly used for collecting data from
                relational databases.
              </p>
              <section className="section" />
            </div>
            <article
              className="nested3"

            >
              <h4

                Adding Source
              </h4>
              <div>
                <p />
                <section className="section">
                  <p />
                </section>
                <section>
                  <ol>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Add</strong> on{" "}
                        <strong>Source</strong> to expand
                        source information.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Enter source name and description, and select{" "}
                        <strong>SQL2DB</strong>
                        for the driver. The system expands the information that
                        needs to be entered for this driver according to the
                        selected driver.{" "}
                      </span>
                      <div>
                        <table
                          id="relational_database_add_origin__table_wsf_3wn_wtb"
                          className="frame-all"
                        >
                          <caption>
                            <span className="table--title-label">
                              Table 21.
                            </span>
                            <span />
                          </caption>
                          <colgroup>

                          </colgroup>
                          <thead>
                            <tr>
                              <th id="relational_database_add_origin__table_wsf_3wn_wtb__entry__1">
                                Parameter
                              </th>

                                Description
                              </th>
                            </tr>
                          </thead>
                          <tbody>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="relational_database_add_origin__table_wsf_3wn_wtb__entry__1">
                                *Server Address
                              </td>

                              <td headers="relational_database_add_origin__table_wsf_3wn_wtb__entry__1">
                                *Database Type
                              </td>
                              <td headers="relational_database_add_origin__table_wsf_3wn_wtb__entry__2">

                        according to the selected source.

### SQL2DB2


<div>
              <p>
                SQL to DB2 driver, mainly used for data acquisition of
                relational database. SQL2DB2 is to access data with table
                structure to X-Collector. MySQL, Oracle, and SQL Server are
                supported. Per data communication, VSTRING is parsed into
                corresponding data type according to the type field TAGTYPE.
              </p>
              <section className="section">
                <p />
              </section>
              <section>
                <div>
                  <div className="p">
                    <span />
                    <br />
                  </div>
                </div>
              </section>

                              <td headers="sql2db2_add_origin__table_gk5_vzn_wtb__entry__1">
                                Q
                              </td>
                              <td headers="sql2db2_add_origin__table_gk5_vzn_wtb__entry__2">
                                INT{" "}
                              </td>
                              <td headers="sql2db2_add_origin__table_gk5_vzn_wtb__entry__3">
                                NUMBER
                              </td>
                              <td headers="sql2db2_add_origin__table_gk5_vzn_wtb__entry__4">
                                Quality code
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="sql2db2_add_origin__table_gk5_vzn_wtb__entry__1">
                                TagType
                              </td>
                              <td headers="sql2db2_add_origin__table_gk5_vzn_wtb__entry__2">
                                INT{" "}
                              </td>
                              <td headers="sql2db2_add_origin__table_gk5_vzn_wtb__entry__3">
                                NUMBER{" "}
                              </td>
                              <td headers="sql2db2_add_origin__table_gk5_vzn_wtb__entry__4">
                                Tag type, value range 0-5, corresponding to data
                                type String/Integer/Long/Float/Double/Bool
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="sql2db2_add_origin__table_gk5_vzn_wtb__entry__1">
                                VInt{" "}
                              </td>
                              <td headers="sql2db2_add_origin__table_gk5_vzn_wtb__entry__2">
                                INT{" "}
                              </td>
                              <td headers="sql2db2_add_origin__table_gk5_vzn_wtb__entry__3">
                                NUMBER{" "}
                              </td>
                              <td headers="sql2db2_add_origin__table_gk5_vzn_wtb__entry__4">
                                -
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="sql2db2_add_origin__table_gk5_vzn_wtb__entry__1">
                                VLong
                              </td>
                              <td headers="sql2db2_add_origin__table_gk5_vzn_wtb__entry__2">
                                BIGINT
                              </td>
                              <td headers="sql2db2_add_origin__table_gk5_vzn_wtb__entry__3">
                                NUMBER{" "}
                              </td>

                                -
                              </td>

                            <tr>
                              <td headers="sql2db2_add_origin__table_gk5_vzn_wtb__entry__1">

                              </td>

                                FLOAT
                              </td>

                                -
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="sql2db2_add_origin__table_gk5_vzn_wtb__entry__1">
                                VDouble
                              </td>
                              <td headers="sql2db2_add_origin__table_gk5_vzn_wtb__entry__2">
                                DOUBLE
                              </td>

                                -
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="sql2db2_add_origin__table_gk5_vzn_wtb__entry__1">
                                VBool{" "}
                              </td>

                                TINYINT{" "}
                              </td>

                                NUMBER

                                -
                              </td>
                            </tr>

                              <td headers="sql2db2_add_origin__table_gk5_vzn_wtb__entry__1">
                                time{" "}
                              </td>

                              </td>

                                -
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                          </tbody>
                        </table>
                      </div>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>Set collect interval to one second. </span>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        After the information is entered, click{" "}
                        <strong>Connection Test</strong>. The
                        configuration is completed if the prompt{" "}
                        <strong>Connection succeeded</strong> pops up.{" "}
                      </span>
                      <div>
                        


:::info


If you are not sure about database information, please check with
                          the database administrator.

:::

</div>
                    </li>
                  </ol>
                </section>
              </div>
            </article>

              id="sql2db2_importing_tag"

                        corresponding to the source.

                        {" "}

                      </span>

                        {" "}

                        according to the selected source.

                        {" "}

                        automatically displays the I/O address.

                        {" "}

                        complete configuration.
                      </span>

## Power Regulations


<div>
            <p />

          </div>
          <article

            aria-labelledby="ariaid-title52"
            id="iec101"
          >
            


### IEC101


<p>
              IEC 101 driver, power system 101 protocol, mainly used to connect
              IEC101 SLAVE.
            </p>
            <article
              className="nested3"
              aria-labelledby="ariaid-title53"
              id="iec101_add_origin"
            >
              <h4 className="topictitle4" id="ariaid-title53">
                Adding Source
              </h4>
              <div>
                <p />
                <section className="section">
                  <p />
                </section>
                <section>
                  <ol>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Add</strong> on{" "}
                        <strong>Source</strong> to expand the
                        source information configuration.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Enter source name and description, and select{" "}
                        <strong>IEC 101</strong>
                        for the driver. The system expands the information that
                        needs to be entered for this driver according to the
                        selected driver.{" "}
                      </span>
                      <div>
                        <table
                          id="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb"
                          className="frame-all"
                        >
                          <caption>
                            <span className="table--title-label">
                              Table 25.{" "}
                            </span>
                            <span>IEC source parameter specification</span>
                          </caption>
                          <colgroup><col style={{ width: "20%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "20%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "60%" }} /></colgroup>
                          <thead>
                            <tr>
                              <th id="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__1">
                                Parameter
                              </th>
                              <th id="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__2">
                                Meaning
                              </th>
                              <th id="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__3">
                                Description
                              </th>
                            </tr>
                          </thead>
                          <tbody>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__1">
                                *Link Address Length
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__2">
                                Link address length
                              </td>
                              <td
                                headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__3"
                                rowSpan={2}
                              >
                                <p>
                                  If the link address length is 1, then the link
                                  address range is 1-255.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  If the link address length is 2, then link
                                  address range is 1-65536.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__1">
                                *Link Address
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__2">
                                Link address field is slave station address
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__1">
                                Update Speed
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__2">
                                Data update speed
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__3">
                                Set update frequency in milliseconds.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__1">
                                *Transmission Reason Length
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__2">
                                Transmission reason
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__3">
                                Byte number of transmission reason (You can
                                choose 1 or 2)
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__1">
                                Public Address Length
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__2">
                                Public address length
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__3">
                                Byte number of public address length (You can
                                choose 1 or 2)
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__1">
                                Info Object Address Length
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__2">
                                Address Length of Info Object
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__3">
                                Byte number of info object address
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__1">
                                Master Channel Settings
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__2">
                                -
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__3">
                                -
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__1">
                                *Serial Port
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__2">
                                Serial port number
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__3">
                                Serial port number of the collector server
                                connected to IEC101 server, fill in the number
                                type, e.g. 1 means COM1.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__1">
                                *Baud Rate
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__2">
                                Baud rate of channel{" "}
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__3">
                                <p>
                                  Baud rate can be set to 110, 150, 300, 600,
                                  1200, 2400, 4800, 9600, 19200, 38400, 57600,
                                  115200.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  The settings must be consistent with the
                                  corresponding parameters on the IEC101 server.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__1">
                                *Parity
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__2">
                                Error checking type of port
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__3">
                                <p>
                                  Optional parameters include the following:
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  None, indicating that no parity bits are added
                                  to the data bits sent from this port.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  Even, indicating that the parity bit should be
                                  set to 1 if the number of 1's in the data bits
                                  is to be even.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  Odd, means that if the number of 1's in the
                                  data bits is odd, the parity bit should be
                                  added.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  Mark, which means that the parity bit is
                                  added, but is always set to 0.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  Space, which means that parity bits are added
                                  but are always set to 1.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  The setting must be the same as the
                                  corresponding parameter on the IEC101 service
                                  side.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__1">
                                Timeout Time
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__2">
                                The maximum waiting time between the command
                                sent by the master and the response
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__3">
                                Unit: ms
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__1">
                                Retry Delay
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__2">
                                Delay time
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__3">
                                Time interval between packet timeout and the
                                next packet.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__1">
                                Number of Retries
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__2">
                                <p>
                                  Number of times to retry sending the command
                                  after the command response timeout.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__3">
                                The default setting is 3 times
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td
                                headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__1"
                                rowSpan={3}
                              >
                                Info Type
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__2">
                                Single point information setting.
                              </td>
                              <td
                                headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__3"
                                rowSpan={3}
                              >
                                Select the corresponding information type, enter
                                the public address (COA), and the COA
                                corresponds to the Slave configuration.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__2">
                                Double point information setting.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec101_add_origin__table_o5m_ycw_xtb__entry__2">
                                Normalized value setting.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                          </tbody>
                        </table>
                      </div>
                    </li>
                  </ol>
                </section>
              </div>
            </article>
            <article
              className="nested3"
              aria-labelledby="ariaid-title54"
              id="iec_101_add_tag"
            >
              <h4 className="topictitle4" id="ariaid-title54">
                Adding Tag
              </h4>
              <div>
                <p />
                <section>
                  <ol>
                    <li>
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Add</strong> to unfold
                        basic properties of tag.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        After the basic property content is input, the system
                        automatically adds the relevant configuration properties
                        for the connection point between tag and the underlying
                        data.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Select tag and enter block offset i.e. select the
                        location of the data; selecting 0 means to read the data
                        from the first place. Click
                        <strong>Save</strong> to complete
                        configuration.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                  </ol>
                </section>
              </div>
            </article>
          </article>

### IEC 103


<div>
              <p>
                IEC 103 driver, power system 103 protocol, used to connect
                IEC103 SLAVE.
              </p>
              <section className="section" />
            </div>
            <article
              className="nested3"
              aria-labelledby="ariaid-title56"
              id="iec103_add_origin"
            >
              <h4 className="topictitle4" id="ariaid-title56">
                Adding Source
              </h4>
              <div>
                <p />
                <section className="section" />
                <section>
                  <ol>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Add</strong> on{" "}
                        <strong>Source</strong> to expand the
                        source information configuration.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Enter source name and description, and select{" "}
                        <strong>IEC 103</strong>
                        for the driver. The system expands the information that
                        needs to be entered for this driver according to the
                        selected driver.{" "}
                      </span>
                      <div>
                        <table
                          id="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb"
                          className="frame-all"
                        >
                          <caption>
                            <span className="table--title-label">
                              Table 26.{" "}
                            </span>
                            <span>IEC 103 source parameter specification</span>
                          </caption>
                          <colgroup><col style={{ width: "20%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "20%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "60%" }} /></colgroup>
                          <thead>
                            <tr>
                              <th id="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__1">
                                Parameter
                              </th>
                              <th id="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__2">
                                Meaning
                              </th>
                              <th id="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__3">
                                Description
                              </th>
                            </tr>
                          </thead>
                          <tbody>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__1">
                                *Link Address
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__2">
                                Link address field is slave station address
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__3">
                                The link address range is 1-255.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__1">
                                *COA{" "}
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__2">
                                Public address of application service data unit{" "}
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__3">
                                COA corresponds to the Slave configuration,
                                ranging from 0-255.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__1">
                                Collect Interval (ms)
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__2">
                                Data acquisition interval frequency
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__3">
                                <p>
                                  Baud rate can be set to 110, 300, 600, 1200,
                                  2400, 4800,9600, 14400, 19200, 38400, 56000,
                                  57600, 115200, 128000, 256000.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  The settings must be consistent with the
                                  corresponding parameters on the IEC103 server.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__1">
                                Master Channel Setting
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__2"></td>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__3"></td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__1">
                                *Serial Port
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__2">
                                Serial port number
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__3">
                                Serial port number of the collector server
                                connected to IEC101 server, fill in the number
                                type, e.g. 1 means COM1
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__1">
                                *Baud Rate
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__2">
                                Baud rate of channel{" "}
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__3">
                                <p>
                                  Baud rate can be set to 110, 150, 300, 600,
                                  1200, 2400, 4800, 9600, 19200, 38400, 57600,
                                  115200.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  The settings must be consistent with the
                                  corresponding parameters on the IEC101 server.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__1">
                                *Parity
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__2">
                                Error checking type of port
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__3">
                                <p>
                                  Optional parameters include the following:
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  None, indicating that no parity bits are added
                                  to the data bits sent from this port.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  Even, indicating that the parity bit should be
                                  set to 1 if the number of 1's in the data bits
                                  is to be even.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  Odd, means that if the number of 1's in the
                                  data bits is odd, the parity bit should be
                                  added.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  Mark, which means that the parity bit is
                                  added, but is always set to 0.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  Space, which means that parity bits are added
                                  but are always set to 1.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  The setting must be the same as the
                                  corresponding parameter on the IEC101 service
                                  side.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__1">
                                *Data Bit
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__2">
                                Number of data bits used in the transmission and
                                reception of each character
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__3">
                                <p>
                                  Optional parameters are 5, 6, 7, 8, and the
                                  default selection is 8.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  The setting must be consistent with the
                                  corresponding parameters of IEC103 server.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__1">
                                Timeout Time
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__2">
                                The maximum waiting time between the command
                                sent by the master and the response
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__3">
                                Default value is 5000ms.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__1">
                                *Stop Bit
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__2">
                                <p>
                                  Transmission time between each character,
                                  measuring by bits/second.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec103_add_origin__table_xbs_wnw_xtb__entry__3">
                                <p>
                                  Optional parameters are 1, 1.5, 2, the default
                                  choice is 1.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  The setting must be the same as the
                                  corresponding parameter on the IEC103 server.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                          </tbody>
                        </table>
                      </div>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Save</strong> to
                        complete configuration.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                  </ol>
                </section>
              </div>
            </article>

                              </td>

                                the information body identifier of the
                                Application Service Data Units (ASDUs).
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec_103_add_tag__table_h3p_j2x_xtb__entry__3">
                                &lt;0-255&gt;
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec_103_add_tag__table_h3p_j2x_xtb__entry__1">
                                Index Number
                              </td>

                              </td>

                                Session
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec104_add_origin__table_r2y_xjx_xtb__entry__3">
                                -
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec104_add_origin__table_r2y_xjx_xtb__entry__1">
                                *Name
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec104_add_origin__table_r2y_xjx_xtb__entry__2">
                                Session Name
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec104_add_origin__table_r2y_xjx_xtb__entry__3">
                                Name under the same session cannot be repeated.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec104_add_origin__table_r2y_xjx_xtb__entry__1">
                                *OA
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec104_add_origin__table_r2y_xjx_xtb__entry__2">
                                Transmitted master station address.
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec104_add_origin__table_r2y_xjx_xtb__entry__3">
                                0 by default
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec104_add_origin__table_r2y_xjx_xtb__entry__1">
                                *Timeout Time
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec104_add_origin__table_r2y_xjx_xtb__entry__2">
                                Timeout Time for channels{" "}
                              </td>
                              <td headers="iec104_add_origin__table_r2y_xjx_xtb__entry__3">
                                Default value is 30000ms. Greyed by default,
                                uneditable.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                          </tbody>
                        </table>
                      </div>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>
                       Public Address </strong>
                        to add sectors and set sector parameters. Sector
                        parameters are listed in the following table.
                      </span>

                            </span>

                                Description

                            <tr>
                              <td headers="iec104_add_origin__table_u3t_nkx_xtb__entry__1">

                                ranging from 0 to 65533.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                          </tbody>
                        </table>
                      </div>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Save</strong> to
                        complete configuration.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                  </ol>
                </section>
              </div>
            </article>
