### CDT


<div>
              <p>
                CDT protocol driver, mainly used to acquire grid data and
                monitor system to manage remote devices.{" "}
              </p>
              <section className="section" />
            </div>
            <article
              className="nested3"
              aria-labelledby="ariaid-title65"
              id="cdt_add_origin"
            >
              <h4 className="topictitle4" id="ariaid-title65">
                Adding Source
              </h4>
              <div>
                <p />
                <section className="section">
                  <p />
                </section>
                <section>
                  <ol>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Add</strong> on{" "}
                        <strong>Source</strong> to expand the
                        source information.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Enter source name and description, and select{" "}
                        <strong>CDT</strong> for the driver.
                        The system expands the information that needs to be
                        entered for this driver according to the selected
                        driver.{" "}
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Channel</strong> to add
                        channel(s) and set related parameters. Parameter
                        specifications are in the following table:
                      </span>
                      <div>
                        <table>
                          <caption>Table 34. Channel parameter specification</caption>
                          <colgroup><col style={{ width: "20%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "20%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "60%" }} /></colgroup>
                          <thead>
                            <tr>
                              <th id="cdt_add_origin__entry__1">Parameter</th>
                              <th id="cdt_add_origin__entry__2">Meaning</th>
                              <th id="cdt_add_origin__entry__3">Description</th>
                            </tr>
                          </thead>
                          <tbody>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__entry__1">
                                Channel
                              </td>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__entry__2">
                                Channel
                              </td>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__entry__3">-</td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__entry__1">*Name</td>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__entry__2">
                                Channel name
                              </td>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__entry__3">
                                Channel name is generated automatically. Default
                                value is suggested.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__entry__1">
                                Description
                              </td>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__entry__2">
                                Description of channels
                              </td>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__entry__3">-</td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__entry__1">*COM</td>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__entry__2">
                                Serial port number
                              </td>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__entry__3">
                                Serial port number of the collector server that
                                establishes connection with CDT server.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__entry__1">
                                *Baud Rate
                              </td>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__entry__2">
                                Baud rate of channel
                              </td>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__entry__3">
                                <p>
                                  Baud rate can be set to 110, 150, 300, 600,
                                  1200, 2400, 4800, 9600, 19200, 38400, 57600,
                                  115200.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  The settings must be consistent with the
                                  corresponding parameters on the IEC101 server.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__entry__1">
                                *Parity
                              </td>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__entry__2">
                                Error checking type of port
                              </td>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__entry__3">
                                <p>
                                  Optional parameters include the following:
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  None, indicating that no parity bits are added
                                  to the data bits sent from this port.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  Even, indicating that the parity bit should be
                                  set to 1 if the number of 1's in the data bits
                                  is to be even.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  Odd, means that if the number of 1's in the
                                  data bits is odd, the parity bit should be
                                  added.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  Mark, which means that the parity bit is
                                  added, but is always set to 0.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  Space, which means that parity bits are added
                                  but are always set to 1.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  The setting must be the same as the
                                  corresponding parameter on the IEC101 service
                                  side.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__entry__1">
                                *Data Bit
                              </td>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__entry__2">
                                Number of data bits used in the transmission and
                                reception of each character
                              </td>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__entry__3">
                                <p>
                                  Optional parameters are 7 or 8, and the
                                  default selection is 8.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  The setting must be consistent with the
                                  corresponding parameters of CDT.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__entry__1">
                                *Stop Bit
                              </td>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__entry__2">
                                <p>
                                  Transmission time between each character,
                                  measuring by bits/second.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__entry__3">
                                <p>
                                  Optional parameters are 1, 2, and the default
                                  choice is 1.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  The setting must be the same as the
                                  corresponding parameter of CDT server.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                          </tbody>
                        </table>
                      </div>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Substation</strong>{" "}
                        under the channel and configure substation. Parameter
                        specifications are as the follow table.{" "}
                      </span>
                      <div>
                        <table
                          id="cdt_add_origin__table_gkt_1sx_xtb"
                          className="frame-all"
                        >
                          <caption>
                            <span className="table--title-label">
                              Table 34.
                            </span>
                            <span>Substation parameter specification</span>
                          </caption>
                          <colgroup><col style={{ width: "20%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "20%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "60%" }} /></colgroup>
                          <thead>
                            <tr>
                              <th id="cdt_add_origin__table_gkt_1sx_xtb__entry__1">
                                Parameter
                              </th>
                              <th id="cdt_add_origin__table_gkt_1sx_xtb__entry__2">
                                Meaning
                              </th>
                              <th id="cdt_add_origin__table_gkt_1sx_xtb__entry__3">
                                Description
                              </th>
                            </tr>
                          </thead>
                          <tbody>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__table_gkt_1sx_xtb__entry__1">
                                *Name
                              </td>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__table_gkt_1sx_xtb__entry__2">
                                Substation name
                              </td>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__table_gkt_1sx_xtb__entry__3">
                                Substation name under the same Channel cannot be
                                repeated.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__table_gkt_1sx_xtb__entry__1">
                                Description
                              </td>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__table_gkt_1sx_xtb__entry__2">
                                Description of substation
                              </td>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__table_gkt_1sx_xtb__entry__3">
                                -
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__table_gkt_1sx_xtb__entry__1">
                                *Substation ID
                              </td>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__table_gkt_1sx_xtb__entry__2">
                                Substation ID
                              </td>
                              <td headers="cdt_add_origin__table_gkt_1sx_xtb__entry__3">
                                The setting must correspond to the parameter of
                                the CDT server, and the setting range is 1~255
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                          </tbody>
                        </table>
                      </div>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Save</strong> to
                        complete configuration.
                      </span>
                      <div>
                        <img
                          id="cdt_add_origin__image_ehl_vq4_n5b"
                          src="https://wordpressfreezonex.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/supCollector/CDT%20substation.png"
                        />
                      </div>
                    </li>
                  </ol>
                </section>
              </div>
            </article>
            <article
              className="nested3"
              aria-labelledby="ariaid-title66"
              id="cdt_add_tag"
            >
              <h4 className="topictitle4" id="ariaid-title66">
                Adding Tag
              </h4>
              <div>
                <p />
                <section className="section" />
                <section>
                  <ol>
                    <li>
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Add</strong> to unfold
                        basic properties of tag.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        After the basic property content is input, the system
                        automatically adds the relevant configuration properties
                        for the connection point between tag and the underlying
                        data.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Select tag (the CDT driver substation to be connected)
                        and function constraint. Select the type to be
                        connected, frame class code, function code and sequence
                        number. You can refer to the corresponding parameters of
                        the CDT server when setting parameters.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                  </ol>
                  <div>
                    <div className="p">
                      <ul id="cdt_add_tag__ul_hh1_c5x_xtb">
                        <li>
                          Type:
                          <p>
                            Parameters selectable include Telemetry,Telemetry,
                            Electric Energy Pulse and SOE. SOE stands for the
                            record of sequence of time.
                          </p>
                          <p>
                            Data type corresponding to remote signalling is
                            Boolean; The data type corresponding to "telemetry"
                            and "electric energy pulse" is the numeric type
                            converted from hexadecimal to decimal; the data type
                            corresponding to SOE is Boolean, and the return
                            value is 1 when the event occurs and 0 when the
                            event does not occur.
                          </p>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                          Frame Class Code：
                          <p>
                            When <strong>Type</strong> is
                            <strong>Telemetry</strong>, the
                            optional parameters are 97, 179 and 194, 97
                            corresponds to frame A, 179 corresponds to frame C
                            and 194 corresponds to frame B.
                          </p>
                          <p>
                            When
                            <strong>Type</strong>is
                            <strong>Teleignalling</strong>,
                            the default parameter is 244.
                          </p>
                          <p>
                            When <strong>Type</strong> is{" "}
                            <strong>
                           Electric Energy Pulse </strong>
                            , the default parameter is 244.
                          </p>
                          <p>
                            When <strong>Type</strong> is
                            <strong>SOE</strong>, the default
                            parameter is 38.
                          </p>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                          {" "}
                          Function Node: Function node stands for the data
                          corresponding to the row in which it is located.{" "}
                          <p>
                            When <strong>Type</strong> is
                            <strong>Telemetry</strong>, the
                            optional parameters are 0 to 127. 0 means the data
                            of telemetry 0.
                          </p>
                          <p>
                            When
                            <strong>Type</strong> is
                            <strong>Teleignalling</strong>,
                            the selectable parameters are 240 to 255, 240 means
                            the data of the first group, each group has 32 data
                            lines; 241 means the data of the second group, and
                            so on.
                          </p>
                          <p>
                            When <strong>Type</strong> selects
                            <strong>
                           Electric Energy Pulse </strong>
                            , the optional parameters are 160 to 223, and 160
                            means the data of electricity 0.
                          </p>
                          <p>
                            When <strong>Type</strong> is
                            <strong>SOE</strong>, the optional
                            parameters are 128 and 129, which indicates the
                            return results corresponding to 80H and 81H, both of
                            which are currently returned.
                          </p>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                          {" "}
                          Sequence Number:
                          <p>
                            When <strong>Type</strong> is
                            <strong>Telemetry</strong>, the
                            optional parameters are 0 and 1, indicating the data
                            for the corresponding column.
                          </p>
                          When
                          <strong>Type</strong> is{" "}
                          <strong>Teleignalling</strong>, The
                          optional parameters are 0 to 31. 0 means the first
                          line of data of each group; for example, the function
                          code is 241, and the sequence number is 0
                          corresponding to the first line of data of the second
                          group, i.e., the 32nd line of data (starting from the
                          0th line).
                          <p>
                            When
                            <strong>Type</strong> is{" "}
                            <strong>
                           Electric Energy Pulse </strong>
                            , the optional parameter is 0.
                          </p>
                          <p>
                            When
                            <strong>Type</strong> is{" "}
                            <strong>SOE</strong>, the optional
                            parameters are 0 to 4095, corresponding to the
                            object number of the server.
                          </p>
                        </li>
                      </ul>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <ol start={4}>
                    <li>
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Save</strong> to
                        complete configuration.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                  </ol>
                </section>
              </div>
            </article>
          </article>
        </article>

                      <div>
                        <table
                          id="r_series_add_tag__table_dpm_cmy_xtb"
                          className="frame-all"

                              Table 39.
                            </span>
                            <span>
                              Parameter specification of R series configurations
                            </span>
                          </caption>

                          <thead>
                            <tr>
                              <th id="r_series_add_tag__table_dpm_cmy_xtb__entry__1">
                                Parameter
                              </th>
                              <th id="r_series_add_tag__table_dpm_cmy_xtb__entry__2">
                                Meaning
                              </th>

                                Specification
                              </th>
                            </tr>
                          </thead>
                          <tbody>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="r_series_add_tag__table_dpm_cmy_xtb__entry__1">
                                *IO Address
                              </td>
                              <td headers="r_series_add_tag__table_dpm_cmy_xtb__entry__2">
                                IO address type
                              </td>
                              <td headers="r_series_add_tag__table_dpm_cmy_xtb__entry__3">
                                <p>D (Data register)</p>
                                <p>AI (input register)</p>
                                <p>AQ (output register)</p>
                                <p>I (Input Relay)</p>
                                <p>Q (output relay)</p>
                                <p>M (Intermediate Relay)</p>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="r_series_add_tag__table_dpm_cmy_xtb__entry__1">
                                *Data Type
                              </td>
                              <td headers="r_series_add_tag__table_dpm_cmy_xtb__entry__2">
                                Data type of tag
                              </td>
                              <td headers="r_series_add_tag__table_dpm_cmy_xtb__entry__3">
                                <p>
                                  IO address type is D/AI/AQ, and the data type
                                  can choose a type other than bool. Bool cannot
                                  be chosen.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  IO address type is I/Q/M, and data type can
                                  only be bool.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="r_series_add_tag__table_dpm_cmy_xtb__entry__1">
                                *Address Offset
                              </td>
                              <td headers="r_series_add_tag__table_dpm_cmy_xtb__entry__2">
                                Address offset
                              </td>
                              <td headers="r_series_add_tag__table_dpm_cmy_xtb__entry__3">
                                Select the offset value, i.e., select the
                                position of the data. Select 0 means to read the
                                data from the first position.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="r_series_add_tag__table_dpm_cmy_xtb__entry__1">
                                *String Length
                              </td>
                              <td headers="r_series_add_tag__table_dpm_cmy_xtb__entry__2">
                                String length
                              </td>
                              <td headers="r_series_add_tag__table_dpm_cmy_xtb__entry__3">
                                Optional string length when string is selected
                                for data format only.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                          </tbody>
                        </table>
                      </div>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Save</strong> to
                        complete configuration.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                  </ol>
                </section>
              </div>

                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Add</strong> on{" "}
                        <strong>Source</strong> to expand the
                        source information configuration.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Enter source name and description, and select{" "}
                        <strong>Mitsubishi CNC</strong> for
                        the driver. The system expands the information that
                        needs to be entered for this driver according to the
                        selected driver.
                      </span>

### A_3C_Format


<p>Connect Mitsubishi PLC via Qna 3C protocol.</p>
            <article
              className="nested3"
              aria-labelledby="ariaid-title86"
              id="a_3c_format_add_origin"
            >
              <h4 className="topictitle4" id="ariaid-title86">
                Adding Source
              </h4>
              <div>
                <p />
                <section>
                  <ol>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Add</strong> on{" "}
                        <strong>Source</strong> to expand the
                        source information configuration.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Enter source name and description, and select{" "}
                        <strong>
                       Mitsubishi A_3C_Format </strong>
                        for the driver. The system expands the information that
                        needs to be entered for this driver according to the
                        selected driver.
                      </span>
                      <div>
                        <table
                          id="a_3c_format_add_origin__table_gm1_pp2_ytb"
                          className="frame-all"
                        >
                          <caption>
                            <span className="table--title-label">
                              Table 44.
                            </span>
                            <span>
                              A_3C_Format source parameter specification
                            </span>
                          </caption>
                          <colgroup><col style={{ width: "20%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "20%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "60%" }} /></colgroup>
                          <thead>
                            <tr>
                              <th id="a_3c_format_add_origin__table_gm1_pp2_ytb__entry__1">
                                Parameter
                              </th>
                              <th id="a_3c_format_add_origin__table_gm1_pp2_ytb__entry__2">
                                Meaning
                              </th>
                              <th id="a_3c_format_add_origin__table_gm1_pp2_ytb__entry__3">
                                Description
                              </th>
                            </tr>
                          </thead>
                          <tbody>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="a_3c_format_add_origin__table_gm1_pp2_ytb__entry__1">
                                Station Number
                              </td>
                              <td headers="a_3c_format_add_origin__table_gm1_pp2_ytb__entry__2">
                                PLC station number
                              </td>
                              <td headers="a_3c_format_add_origin__table_gm1_pp2_ytb__entry__3">
                                PLC address, 0 by default
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="a_3c_format_add_origin__table_gm1_pp2_ytb__entry__1">
                                Master Channel Settings
                              </td>
                              <td headers="a_3c_format_add_origin__table_gm1_pp2_ytb__entry__2">
                                -
                              </td>
                              <td headers="a_3c_format_add_origin__table_gm1_pp2_ytb__entry__3">
                                -
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="a_3c_format_add_origin__table_gm1_pp2_ytb__entry__1">
                                Serial Port
                              </td>
                              <td headers="a_3c_format_add_origin__table_gm1_pp2_ytb__entry__2">
                                Serial port number
                              </td>
                              <td headers="a_3c_format_add_origin__table_gm1_pp2_ytb__entry__3">
                                Serial port number of the collector server that
                                establishes connection with the PLC.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="a_3c_format_add_origin__table_gm1_pp2_ytb__entry__1">
                                *Baud Rate
                              </td>
                              <td headers="a_3c_format_add_origin__table_gm1_pp2_ytb__entry__2">
                                Baud rate of channel{" "}
                              </td>
                              <td headers="a_3c_format_add_origin__table_gm1_pp2_ytb__entry__3">
                                <p>
                                  Baud rate can be set to 110, 300, 600, 1200,
                                  2400, 4800, 9600, 14400, 19200, 38400, 56000,
                                  57600, 115200, 128000, 256000.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  The settings must be consistent with the
                                  corresponding parameters of IEC101 server.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="a_3c_format_add_origin__table_gm1_pp2_ytb__entry__1">
                                Data Bit
                              </td>
                              <td headers="a_3c_format_add_origin__table_gm1_pp2_ytb__entry__2">
                                Data bit used for transmitting and receiving
                                each character.
                              </td>
                              <td headers="a_3c_format_add_origin__table_gm1_pp2_ytb__entry__3">
                                The optional parameter is 7 or 8, and the
                                default is 8.
                                <p>
                                  The settings must be consistent with the
                                  parameter corresponding to PLC server.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="a_3c_format_add_origin__table_gm1_pp2_ytb__entry__1">
                                Stop Bit
                              </td>
                              <td headers="a_3c_format_add_origin__table_gm1_pp2_ytb__entry__2">
                                Time between transmission of each character,
                                measured in bits per second.
                              </td>
                              <td headers="a_3c_format_add_origin__table_gm1_pp2_ytb__entry__3">
                                The optional parameters are 1, 1.5 and 2, and
                                the default is 1. The settings must be
                                consistent with the parameters corresponding to
                                PLC.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="a_3c_format_add_origin__table_gm1_pp2_ytb__entry__1">
                                Parity
                              </td>
                              <td headers="a_3c_format_add_origin__table_gm1_pp2_ytb__entry__2">
                                Type of error checking for the port.
                              </td>
                              <td headers="a_3c_format_add_origin__table_gm1_pp2_ytb__entry__3">
                                <p>
                                  Optional parameters include the following:
                                </p>
                                <div className="p">
                                  <ul id="a_3c_format_add_origin__ul_khz_1t2_ytb">
                                    <li>
                                      None, indicating that no parity bit is
                                      added to data bits sent from this port.
                                    </li>
                                    <li>
                                      Odd, indicating that if the number of 1's
                                      in the data bits is to be odd. The parity
                                      bit should be added.{" "}
                                    </li>
                                    <li>
                                      Even, indicating that if the number of 1's
                                      in the data bits is to be even. The parity
                                      bit should be set to 1.
                                    </li>
                                    <li>
                                      Mark, meaning adding parity bit. (always
                                      set to 0).
                                    </li>
                                    <li>
                                      {" "}
                                      Space, meaning adding parity bit (always
                                      set to 1).
                                    </li>
                                    <li>
                                      {" "}
                                      The settings must be consistent with the
                                      parameters corresponding to the PLC.
                                    </li>
                                  </ul>
                                </div>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                          </tbody>
                        </table>
                      </div>
                    </li>
                  </ol>
                </section>
              </div>
            </article>
            <article
              className="nested3"
              aria-labelledby="ariaid-title87"
              id="a_3c_format_add_tag"
            >
              <h4 className="topictitle4" id="ariaid-title87">
                Adding Tag
              </h4>
              <div>
                <p>
                  For details, see{" "}
                  <a href="#a_1e_add_tag__title_tg3_l1j_25b">
                    Adding Tag
                  </a>{" "}
                  .
                </p>
                <section className="section" />
              </div>
            </article>
          </article>

            className="nested2"
            aria-labelledby="ariaid-title88"
            id="a_3c_tcp"

### Fx_Links_485

                              </td>
                              <td headers="fx_links_485_add_origin__table_uxx_1v2_ytb__entry__3">
                                PLC address, 0 by default.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="fx_links_485_add_origin__table_uxx_1v2_ytb__entry__1">
                                Timeout Time
                              </td>
                              <td headers="fx_links_485_add_origin__table_uxx_1v2_ytb__entry__2">
                                Maximum wait time of device connection timeout.
                              </td>
                              <td headers="fx_links_485_add_origin__table_uxx_1v2_ytb__entry__3">
                                0 by default. Unit: ms.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="fx_links_485_add_origin__table_uxx_1v2_ytb__entry__1">
                                Parity
                              </td>
                              <td headers="fx_links_485_add_origin__table_uxx_1v2_ytb__entry__2">
                                Device supports checksum varification.
                              </td>
                              <td headers="fx_links_485_add_origin__table_uxx_1v2_ytb__entry__3">
                                You can select Yes or No.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="fx_links_485_add_origin__table_uxx_1v2_ytb__entry__1">
                                Master Channel Settings
                              </td>
                              <td headers="fx_links_485_add_origin__table_uxx_1v2_ytb__entry__2">
                                -
                              </td>
                              <td headers="fx_links_485_add_origin__table_uxx_1v2_ytb__entry__3">
                                -
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="fx_links_485_add_origin__table_uxx_1v2_ytb__entry__1">
                                Serial Port
                              </td>
                              <td headers="fx_links_485_add_origin__table_uxx_1v2_ytb__entry__2">
                                Serial port number
                              </td>
                              <td headers="fx_links_485_add_origin__table_uxx_1v2_ytb__entry__3">
                                Serial port number of the collector server that
                                establishes connection with the PLC.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="fx_links_485_add_origin__table_uxx_1v2_ytb__entry__1">
                                *Baud Rate
                              </td>
                              <td headers="fx_links_485_add_origin__table_uxx_1v2_ytb__entry__2">
                                Baud rate of channel{" "}
                              </td>
                              <td headers="fx_links_485_add_origin__table_uxx_1v2_ytb__entry__3">
                                <p>
                                  Baud rate can be set to 110, 300, 600, 1200,
                                  2400, 4800, 9600, 14400, 19200, 38400, 56000,
                                  57600, 115200, 128000, 256000.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  The settings must be consistent with the
                                  corresponding parameters on the IEC101 server.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="fx_links_485_add_origin__table_uxx_1v2_ytb__entry__1">
                                Data Bit
                              </td>
                              <td headers="fx_links_485_add_origin__table_uxx_1v2_ytb__entry__2">
                                Data bit used for transmitting and receiving
                                each character.
                              </td>
                              <td headers="fx_links_485_add_origin__table_uxx_1v2_ytb__entry__3">
                                The optional parameter is 7 or 8, and the
                                default selection is 8 The setting must be
                                consistent with the parameter corresponding to
                                the PLC server.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="fx_links_485_add_origin__table_uxx_1v2_ytb__entry__1">
                                Stop Bit
                              </td>
                              <td headers="fx_links_485_add_origin__table_uxx_1v2_ytb__entry__2">
                                Time between transmission of each character,
                                measured in bits per second.
                              </td>
                              <td headers="fx_links_485_add_origin__table_uxx_1v2_ytb__entry__3">
                                The optional parameters are 1, 1.5 and 2, and
                                the default selection is 1. The settings must be
                                consistent with the parameters corresponding to
                                the PLC.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="fx_links_485_add_origin__table_uxx_1v2_ytb__entry__1">
                                Parity
                              </td>
                              <td headers="fx_links_485_add_origin__table_uxx_1v2_ytb__entry__2">
                                Type of error checking for the port.
                              </td>
                              <td headers="fx_links_485_add_origin__table_uxx_1v2_ytb__entry__3">
                                <p>Optional parameters include:</p>
                                <div className="p">
                                  <ul id="fx_links_485_add_origin__ul_khz_1t2_ytb">
                                    <li>
                                      None, indicating that no parity bit is
                                      added to data bits sent from this port.
                                    </li>
                                    <li>
                                      Odd, indicating that if the number of 1's
                                      in the data bits is to be odd, the parity
                                      bit should be added.
                                    </li>
                                    <li>
                                      Even, indicating that if the number of 1's
                                      in the data bits is to be even, the parity
                                      bit should be set to 1.{" "}
                                    </li>
                                    <li>
                                      Mark, means adding parity bit, but always
                                      set to 0.{" "}
                                    </li>
                                    <li>
                                      {" "}
                                      Space, means adding parity bit, but always
                                      set to 1.
                                    </li>
                                    <li>
                                      {" "}
                                      The settings must be consistent with the
                                      parameters corresponding to the PLC.
                                    </li>
                                  </ul>
                                </div>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                          </tbody>
                        </table>
                      </div>
                    </li>
                  </ol>
                </section>
              </div>
            </article>

### Fx_Serial_TCP

                              headers="cnc_tcp_add_origin__table_yvy_f54_n5b__entry__1"
                            >
                              Timeout Time
                            </td>
                            <td
                              className="colsep-1 rowsep-1"

                            </td>
                            <td

                            >
                              5000 by default. Unit: ms
                            </td>
                          </tr>
                        </tbody>
                      </table>
                    </div>
                  </li>
                </ol>
              </section>
            </div>

## Simens


<div>
            <p />
            <section className="section" />
          </div>
          <article
            className="nested2"
            aria-labelledby="simens_profinet__title_v3n_zmj_25b"
            id="simens_profinet"
          >
            


### Profinet


<p>
              Connect PLC of 808D series, 828D series, 828Dsl series via
              Profinet protocol (device must have 127 or 130 network port), 840D
              series (implemented via httpDDE protocol).{" "}
            </p>

### HostLink_TCP


<p>
              Connect PLC of Omron through the network port via HostLink
              protocol.
            </p>

                                Bit offset
                              </td>

                                Bit offset can only be selected when data type
                                is bool, ranging from 0-7. Selecting 0 means to

                                by default. Unit: ms
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                          </tbody>
                        </table>
                      </div>
                    </li>
                  </ol>
                </section>
              </div>
            </article>
            <article

                                Data stores code
                              </td>
                              <td headers="fins_udp_add_tag__table_btv_bxm_ytb__entry__3">
                                <p>A（Auxiliary Bit Area）</p>
                                <p>C（CIO Area）</p>
                                <p>D（Data Memory Area）</p>

                              </td>
                            </tr>

                              <td headers="fins_udp_add_tag__table_btv_bxm_ytb__entry__1">
                                *Data Type
                              </td>
                              <td headers="fins_udp_add_tag__table_btv_bxm_ytb__entry__2">
                                Data type that has been read.
                              </td>

                                the register data
                              </td>

                              </td>

                                Bit Offset
                              </td>

                                Bit offset
                              </td>
                              <td headers="fins_udp_add_tag__table_btv_bxm_ytb__entry__3">
                                Bit offset can only be selected when data type
                                is bool, ranging from 0-7. Selecting 0 means to
                                read from the first bit.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="fins_udp_add_tag__table_btv_bxm_ytb__entry__1">

                              </td>

                                is byte, ranging from 0-1.{" "}
                              </td>

                              </td>

                                String Length can only be selected when the data
                                type is string.{" "}
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                          </tbody>
                        </table>
                      </div>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Save</strong> to
                        complete configuration.
                      </span>

### Host_Link_COM


<p>Connect Omron PLC via HostLink protocol. </p>
            <article
              className="nested3"
              aria-labelledby="hostlink_add_origin__title_l11_hnj_25b"
              id="hostlink_add_origin"
            >
              <h4
                className="topictitle4"
                id="hostlink_add_origin__title_l11_hnj_25b"
              >
                Adding Source
              </h4>
              <div>
                <p />
                <section>
                  <ol>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Click <strong>Add</strong> on{" "}
                        <strong>Source</strong> to expand
                        source information.
                      </span>
                    </li>
                    <li className="stepexpand">
                      <span>
                        {" "}
                        Enter source name and description, and select
                        <strong>Host_Link_COM</strong> for the
                        driver. The system expands the information that needs to
                        be entered for this driver according to the selected
                        driver name.
                      </span>
                      <div>
                        <table
                          id="hostlink_add_origin__table_skq_51n_ytb"
                          className="frame-all"
                        >
                          <caption>
                            <span className="table--title-label">
                              Table 68.
                            </span>
                            <span>
                              Host_Link_COM source parameter specification
                            </span>
                          </caption>
                          <colgroup><col style={{ width: "20%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "20%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "60%" }} /></colgroup>
                          <thead>
                            <tr>
                              <th id="hostlink_add_origin__table_skq_51n_ytb__entry__1">
                                Parameter
                              </th>
                              <th id="hostlink_add_origin__table_skq_51n_ytb__entry__2">
                                Meaning
                              </th>
                              <th id="hostlink_add_origin__table_skq_51n_ytb__entry__3">
                                Specification
                              </th>
                            </tr>
                          </thead>
                          <tbody>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="hostlink_add_origin__table_skq_51n_ytb__entry__1">
                                Station Number
                              </td>
                              <td headers="hostlink_add_origin__table_skq_51n_ytb__entry__2">
                                PLC station number
                              </td>
                              <td headers="hostlink_add_origin__table_skq_51n_ytb__entry__3">
                                PLC address, 0 by default
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="hostlink_add_origin__table_skq_51n_ytb__entry__1">
                                Main Channel Settings
                              </td>
                              <td headers="hostlink_add_origin__table_skq_51n_ytb__entry__2"></td>
                              <td headers="hostlink_add_origin__table_skq_51n_ytb__entry__3"></td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="hostlink_add_origin__table_skq_51n_ytb__entry__1">
                                Serial Port
                              </td>
                              <td headers="hostlink_add_origin__table_skq_51n_ytb__entry__2">
                                Serial port number
                              </td>
                              <td headers="hostlink_add_origin__table_skq_51n_ytb__entry__3">
                                Serial port number of the collector server that
                                establishes connection with the PLC
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="hostlink_add_origin__table_skq_51n_ytb__entry__1">
                                *Baud Rate
                              </td>
                              <td headers="hostlink_add_origin__table_skq_51n_ytb__entry__2">
                                Baud rate of channel{" "}
                              </td>
                              <td headers="hostlink_add_origin__table_skq_51n_ytb__entry__3">
                                <p>
                                  Baud rate can be set to 110, 300, 600, 1200,
                                  2400, 4800, 9600, 14400, 19200, 38400, 56000,
                                  57600, 115200, 128000, 256000.
                                </p>
                                <p>
                                  The settings must be consistent with the
                                  corresponding parameters on the IEC101 server.
                                </p>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="hostlink_add_origin__table_skq_51n_ytb__entry__1">
                                Data bit
                              </td>
                              <td headers="hostlink_add_origin__table_skq_51n_ytb__entry__2">
                                Data bit used for transmitting and receiving
                                each character
                              </td>
                              <td headers="hostlink_add_origin__table_skq_51n_ytb__entry__3">
                                The optional parameter is 7 or 8, and the
                                default selection is 8 The setting must be
                                consistent with the parameter corresponding to
                                the PLC server.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="hostlink_add_origin__table_skq_51n_ytb__entry__1">
                                Stop Bit
                              </td>
                              <td headers="hostlink_add_origin__table_skq_51n_ytb__entry__2">
                                Time between transmission of each character,
                                measured in bits per second
                              </td>
                              <td headers="hostlink_add_origin__table_skq_51n_ytb__entry__3">
                                The optional parameters are 1, 1.5 and 2, and
                                the default selection is 1. The settings must be
                                consistent with the parameters corresponding to
                                the PLC.
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                              <td headers="hostlink_add_origin__table_skq_51n_ytb__entry__1">
                                Parity
                              </td>
                              <td headers="hostlink_add_origin__table_skq_51n_ytb__entry__2">
                                Type of error checking for the port
                              </td>
                              <td headers="hostlink_add_origin__table_skq_51n_ytb__entry__3">
                                <p>Optional parameters include:</p>
                                <div className="p">
                                  <ul id="hostlink_add_origin__ul_khz_1t2_ytb">
                                    <li>
                                      None, indicating that no parity bit is
                                      added to data bits sent from this port.
                                    </li>
                                    <li>
                                      Odd, indicating that if the number of 1's
                                      in the data bits is to be odd, the parity
                                      bit should be added.
                                    </li>
                                    <li>
                                      Even, indicating that if the number of 1's
                                      in the data bits is to be even, the parity
                                      bit should be set to 1.
                                    </li>
                                    <li>
                                      Mark, means adding parity bit, but always
                                      set to 0.{" "}
                                    </li>
                                    <li>
                                      {" "}
                                      Space, means adding parity bit, but always
                                      set to 1
                                    </li>
                                    <li>
                                      {" "}
                                      The settings must be consistent with the
                                      parameters corresponding to the PLC.
                                    </li>
                                  </ul>
                                </div>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                          </tbody>
                        </table>
                      </div>
                    </li>
                  </ol>
                </section>
              </div>
            </article>
            <article
              className="nested3"
              aria-labelledby="host_link_com_add_tag__title_tsg_hnj_25b"
              id="host_link_com_add_tag"
            >
              <h4
                className="topictitle4"
                id="host_link_com_add_tag__title_tsg_hnj_25b"
              >
                Adding Tag
              </h4>
              <p>
                For details, see{" "}
                <a href="#fins_udp_add_tag__title_hrj_gnj_25b">
                  Adding Tag
                </a>
                .
              </p>
            </article>
          </article>
        </article>

## Haas

                      driver name.

                                    party's serial port.

                          <span>AB_DF1 parameter specification</span>
                        </caption>
                        <colgroup><col style={{ width: "20%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "20%" }} />
                            <col style={{ width: "60%" }} /></colgroup>
                        <thead>
                          <tr>
                            <th id="rock_add_tag__table_a4x_3nl_15b__entry__1">
                              Parameter
                            </th>
                            <th id="rock_add_tag__table_a4x_3nl_15b__entry__2">
                              Meaning
                            </th>
                            <th id="rock_add_tag__table_a4x_3nl_15b__entry__3">
                              Specification
                            </th>
                          </tr>
                        </thead>
                        <tbody>
                          <tr>
                            <td headers="rock_add_tag__table_a4x_3nl_15b__entry__1">
                              *Select Tag
                            </td>
                            <td headers="rock_add_tag__table_a4x_3nl_15b__entry__2">
                              Data file
                            </td>
                            <td headers="rock_add_tag__table_a4x_3nl_15b__entry__3">
                              <p>O0: Output</p>
                              <p>I1: Input</p>
                              <p>S2: Status</p>
                              <p>B3: Binary</p>
                              <p>T4: Timer</p>
                              <p>C5: Counter</p>
                              <p>R6: Control</p>
                              <p>N7: Integer number</p>
                              <p>F8: Floating point number</p>
                            </td>
                          </tr>
                          <tr>
                            <td headers="rock_add_tag__table_a4x_3nl_15b__entry__1">
                              *Address
                            </td>
                            <td headers="rock_add_tag__table_a4x_3nl_15b__entry__2">
                              Data file address
                            </td>
                            <td headers="rock_add_tag__table_a4x_3nl_15b__entry__3">
                              -
                            </td>
                          </tr>
                          <tr>
                            <td headers="rock_add_tag__table_a4x_3nl_15b__entry__1">
                              Data Type
                            </td>
                            <td headers="rock_add_tag__table_a4x_3nl_15b__entry__2">
                              Data type
                            </td>
                            <td headers="rock_add_tag__table_a4x_3nl_15b__entry__3">
                              <p>
                                Data type of data source, forward/reverse order,
                                byte swap, etc.
                              </p>
                              <p>Bool: bit setting, 0-15</p>
                              <p>Short/unshort: AB/BA</p>
                              <p>Long/unlong/float: ABCD/CDBA/BADC/DCBA</p>
                              <p>Byte/char: A/B</p>
                              <p>Double: asc/decs</p>
                            </td>
                          </tr>
                        </tbody>
                      </table>
                    </div>
                  </li>
                  <li className="stepexpand">
                    <span>
                      {" "}
                      Click <strong>Save</strong> to complete
                      configuration.
                    </span>
                  </li>
                </ol>
              </section>
            </div>
          </article>

## Network Protocol


<p>
            Simple Network Management Protocol&nbsp;(SNMP) is an&nbsp;Internet
            Standard&nbsp;protocol for managing network nodes (servers,
            workstations, routers, switches, HUBS, etc.) on IP networks. It is
            an application layer protocol.
          </p>
          <article
            className="nested2"
            aria-labelledby="snmp_add_origin__title_anb_nnj_25b"
            id="snmp_add_origin"
          >
            <h3 className="topictitle3" id="snmp_add_origin__title_anb_nnj_25b">
              Adding Source
            </h3>

                <ol>
                  <li className="stepexpand">
                    <span>
                      {" "}
                      Click <strong>Add</strong> on{" "}
                      <strong>Source</strong> page to expand
                      source information.
                    </span>
                  </li>
                  <li className="stepexpand">
                    <span>
                      {" "}
                      Enter source name and description, and select{" "}
                      <strong>SNMP</strong> for the driver.
                      The system expands the information that needs to be
                      entered for this driver according to the selected driver.
                    </span>

                            </td>

                            </td>

                              Configure data acquisition cycle, unit: ms. 1000
                              by default.
                            </td>

                      <strong>Save</strong> to complete
                      configuration.

### RTSP


<div>
              <p />
              <section className="section">
                <p>
                  Any video devices and services that conform to the RTSP
                  protocol can be accessed through the RTSP driver.
                </p>
              </section>
              <section>
                <ol>
                  <li>
                    <span>
                      Click <strong>Add </strong> on the
                      Video Collector to expand video source configuration.
                    </span>
                  </li>
                  <li>
                    <span>
                      Enter the name, alias, and source description, then select
                      RTSP for the video type. The system expands the
                      information that needs to be entered for this driver based
                      on the selected video type.{" "}
                    </span>
                  </li>
                </ol>

### HCNETSDK


<div>

                    </span>

                <div>
                  <table>
                    <caption>
                      <span className="table--title-label">Table 81. </span>
                      <span>Parameter specification</span>

                            <col style={{ width: "20%" }} />

                          video according to your needs.{" "}
                        </td>
                      </tr>

                  <li>
